Free Talk

A Word or Two 175

— Qiushui

Women obtain their self-judgment from the mirror, while men obtain their self-judgment from the eyes of other women.

▲ If the men in the world could put all the energy and courage they use on women into their careers, then the world could have many more millionaires and important figures.

▲ A modern woman will never be afraid when she gets married, because if she wants to marry and cannot be happy, then after a divorce, she can at least taste a little happiness.

▲ Modern youth need a woman who loves him but does not bind him and does not need a wife who can passionately love him but at the same time makes his actions inconvenient.

▲ When a man and a woman are sitting and chatting casually, and the woman hears the man tell a joke and laughs so hard that her whole body is shaking for a long time, then they already have the possibility of getting married. However, the man sometimes still does not understand the reason.

▲ When suffering a huge wound in love, wisdom is a plaster, philosophy is a fragrant oil, and time is a painkiller. Once all three are available, the pain is lost.

▲ Men under the age of thirty-five tremble when they think of marriage, like a dog seeing a rope.

▲ When falling deeply and passionately in love, the capacity to enjoy happiness increases proportionally, but the opportunity to enjoy happiness also decreases proportionally.

▲ If all the women in the world want to stop their husbands from wandering outside and not wanting to go home, you will be greatly disappointed, because this kind of thing is impossible to save, unless it is time, luck, death, divorce, and patience.

▲ Ordinary men find it very difficult to understand the changes in women's psychology, which is as incomprehensible to us as the structure of wireless telegraphy.

Tales of a Sea Traveler 176

— Chen Boying

I have a friend, Mr. Shen, who has recently returned from overseas, having traveled on the President Grant, a ship of the Dollar Steamship Company. After we met and exchanged pleasantries, I asked if he had any interesting news from the Western countries that he could share with me. My friend said, "There are many things, but let me first talk about this ship. The owner of this ship is Robert Dollar, an American. He originally made his living growing sweet potatoes and had no other property, only two mountains, which were entirely planted with sweet potatoes. Once they matured, he sold them to other provinces. Later, the production volume increased day by day, and sales also expanded. He hired steamships to transport them. At that time, there was only a steamship company run by the government, which charged exorbitant freight rates and increased them from time to time. Mr. Dollar calculated his annual profit and found it to be very small. He realized that his hard work was only benefiting the steamship company. So, he devised a method to resist this. He sold one of his mountains and used the funds to build a steamship. In addition to transporting sweet potatoes, he also carried passengers and cargo, charging lower rates than the government-run company. People flocked to him, and he was overwhelmed with business. He then sold his other mountain and used the proceeds, plus the profit he had made, to build a larger steamship to specialize in the shipping business, no longer being a sweet potato merchant. Years later, with the surplus, he built more steamships. By today, there are branch offices established in all commercial ports around the world. He also established world-class liners to circumnavigate the globe, with a steamship sailing from each commercial port every week. One can imagine the large number of ships he has. Therefore, today's Dollar is truly a giant in the shipping industry."

A Record of the Liyun Study 177

— Zhi Zheng

Liyun Study is the new residence of Li Yunliang, the head of the business department of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and his wife, Ms. Meng Yun Chia. The study is located in Chenghe Village on Fuxu Road. A corner of a painted building, it is exquisitely elegant. The arrangement of the hall is particularly beautiful. On the wall, in addition to a pair of mandarin ducks, are the honors that Mr. Li has received over the years for his service to society, as well as the scrolls presented by various dignitaries during his wedding. These fragments of silk are precious. The study is located on the third floor, facing a famous garden. Windows on three sides are covered with willow branches, creating a delicate view. There are many books in the middle. There are inscriptions on the Liyun Study and poems exchanged between the couple, which are refined and worth reading. The host is diligent in serving the party and the country, and the hostess is devoted to education. In their leisure time, they play with their young children. A happy atmosphere permeates the surroundings. Everyone who sees them praises them as a model of true beauty and goodness.

Afterglows Amidst the Celebratory Sounds 178

— Wang Meiyu

Shou Juan invited me to a feast at his residence, the Juan Nest, on the occasion of the Double Tenth celebration. (Note: Juan Nest is Shou Juan's residence.) The guests included those who had just returned from travels to Europe and the West, who spoke in detail about various friendly countries, providing valuable insights. This gentleman is now recording these insights in daily installments on the left side of this discussion column. I will not repeat them. (Note: This gentleman is Mr. Wang Yachen.) After the banquet at 3 p.m., I drove past the Great World and returned to the Baimao Pavilion for a short rest. Suddenly, I received a wedding invitation. It was addressed with "Tea and refreshments will be served at 4 p.m. on the 13th of the tenth month of the national calendar." It was co-signed by the wedding couple, He Songqing and Li Shuqiu. Below Songqing's name was added the phrase "second son of Yuan Fu." This was a fellow member of the Huiwen Society in Suzhou forty years ago. I went to congratulate him as agreed yesterday. What I saw and heard can serve as an afterglow of the Double Tenth celebration. I record it as follows:

▲ Double Tenth, Double Tenth: The He family rents a house near the old Daoguan Street in the city. The house is still spacious. In the middle of the main hall, a silk scroll is hung high, with the words "Double Tenth" written repeatedly in glittering gold. A guest, dressed in Western clothes and leather shoes, smiled at the crowd and said, "What a pity! The wedding date is three days after the National Day." Another guest replied seriously, "No. There is only one Double Tenth in a year. However, the national enthusiasm has the words 'Double Tenth' engraved in the hearts of the people every day." Xu Geng: During the national music, the officiant delivered a speech, then turned around, pointed to the silk scroll, and said to the guests, "Ladies and gentlemen, do you know the subtle meaning of 'Double Tenth, Double Tenth'? Ms. Shuqiu's age, according to the national calendar, is exactly twenty years old. The initial basis for the love between Mr. Songqing and Ms. Shuqiu began when they were both ten years old. So, I repeat it to clarify it." All the guests applauded. The two guests who had exchanged opinions earlier seemed to be lost in thought.

▲ Seeing Benevolence, Seeing Wisdom: The He family's wedding only served tea and refreshments. The guests did not mind its simplicity. The two newlyweds came out and paid their respects to the guests. The officiant asked the guests to talk about the happy events of the Double Tenth Festival since the founding of the Republic. Everyone presented their views, which were full of patriotic ideas. A female guest stood up and reported, "During the Double Tenth Festival of the twelfth year of the Republic, my husband was in Paris. He fell in love with a dancer in that city. I took an open-minded approach, and my husband loved and respected me even more." The guests laughed. I silently recalled the banquet at the Juan Nest, where I heard that the couple Yachen were admired by foreigners. How could this be compared with this? The same Double Tenth, the two newlyweds and this female guest also have a sense of seeing benevolence and seeing wisdom. I append this as an afterglow to my writing.

A Record of the Shoe-Stealing Rat 179

— Qian Xiao

In our town, there is a rogue named Li. He is from a once-noble family but has squandered his wealth through gambling. He has retreated to associating with vagrants and beggars. He has mastered the art of opening boxes and stealing shoes. He especially likes to steal women's high-heeled shoes. His technique of stealing shoes is unpredictable. Shi Qian and Bai Sheng in the Water Margin are probably no more than that. Because the townsfolk think he resembles a rat, they call him the Shoe-Stealing Rat.

Except for the first and fifteenth days of the first month of the lunar calendar, the Shoe-Stealing Rat steals more than ten pairs of shoes every day. He hides them in the big bucket on the flagpole in front of the town temple. No one knows. Every ten days, he examines all the various cloth shoes and leather shoes he has stolen. Those that are broken, old, or smelly are thrown into the dung pit east of the temple. Those that are intact and new in color are wrapped in paper and taken to the city for sale. In the middle of April this spring, a strong wind blew. The flagpole in front of the temple suddenly broke. The bucket fell to the ground and shattered. The shoes also fell down one after another, like butterflies fluttering. The townsfolk flocked to watch, and they realized that this bucket was the Shoe-Stealing Rat's shoe storage. They sighed that his idea was fantastic and praised it. Because his stolen goods were exposed, the Shoe-Stealing Rat was envied by heaven. So, he relocated and sought another mysterious lair to be his shoe storage.

Last month, Mr. Gu, the principal of a certain elementary school, married Ms. Shen. Ms. Shen is the daughter of a wealthy gentleman. She loves to dress up. Her clothes are fashionable and extremely luxurious. Even for a pair of shoes, she spends more than ten gold coins. Therefore, she is most coveted by the Shoe-Stealing Rat. She has lost shoes several times in a year. Although she tries her best to protect them and takes strict precautions, it is ineffective. On the night of her wedding, fearing that her gold-embroidered leather shoes would disappear again, she asked a bridesmaid to sleep with the shoe box in her arms, intending to protect them. When the bridesmaid woke up at dawn, she saw that the shoe box in her arms was still the same. She happily reported to the bride, "Miss, you are very lucky. This time, the Shoe-Stealing Rat worked in vain and could not use his skills." The bride was secretly happy when she heard this. She untied the rope and opened the lid, intending to put them on. But the contents of the box were no longer the real thing. Instead, there was a bow shoe only three inches long, like something belonging to an old woman, and it was broken and tattered. Ms. Shen was stunned when she saw this. The bridesmaid, who had the mission of protecting the shoes while sleeping with the box in her arms, was so frightened that she almost lost her complexion.

Also, my relative, Ms. Zhou, once lost her shoes. They were unexpectedly recovered. The matter was quite interesting. I record it as follows. Ms. Zhou went to the city for business. She saw countless leather shoes in a small shop, marked with "Special Discount, Half Price According to Size." She spent three yuan to buy a pair. The shoes were very delicate, and Ms. Zhou treasured them. Less than ten days after returning to her village, she was again targeted by the Shoe-Stealing Rat, and the shoes disappeared. She was distressed. But only one night later, the shoes were suddenly found on the toilet lid. Attached to the shoes was a note that read, "This has passed through my hands. Is it from a certain store?" Later, Ms. Zhou investigated. These shoes were indeed stolen goods, originally belonging to her classmate, Ms. Qian, and were stolen last year.

An Account of an Italian Art Investigation (5) 180

— Wang Yachen

Giotto was born in 1266 and died in 1337. He was a student of Giovanni Cimabue, a great painter of the early Renaissance. He and his teacher were the pioneers of the Renaissance. Giotto was originally a shepherd boy in his youth. One day, Giotto drew a sheep on a stone wall and was appreciated by Cimabue, who then taught him. Later, he became a great master of a generation. Most of the church's artworks are Giotto's religious frescoes. He was originally an interpreter of Christian legends, so his pictures tend to focus on formal depictions. His technique is slightly stagnant, and his perspective is also incomplete. However, the purity of the characters he depicts is better than the later masterpieces of the Renaissance.

Few of Cimabue's paintings have been passed down. There are several pieces of his handmade clay relief sculptures in this church. In the early Italian Renaissance, there was a type of clay relief sculpture that is still specially recorded in art history, because there was an amazing skill in clay relief sculpture at that time. Cimabue was one of the first people to invent clay relief sculpture. After seeing Giotto's frescoes, I entered the Crocifisso Chapel. On both sides of the main hall of the chapel are more than ten tombs of famous Italians throughout history. Among them, two tombs particularly caught my attention. One is of the literary giant Dante, and the other is of the great artist Michelangelo.

(6) San Marco Church: There are many frescoes in this church. Among them, there is a picture of "The Descent of the Angel," which is the work of Fra Angelico, a great painter of the early Renaissance. This painting is on the wall of the corridor on the second floor of the church.

Fra Angelico was a religious believer who was good at describing the retribution of good and evil. He was quite famous at the time. His brushwork is extremely strong in the painting, and the color is also gorgeous. In addition to the large frescoes in the temple, there are also pictures of the deeds of Jesus. Each picture is displayed in a small room, totaling more than ten rooms. On the opposite side, there are also dozens of rooms, which contain the frescoes of Savonarola. Savonarola was a great painter after Fra Angelico. He was also a religious believer. His technique is roughly the same. He was highly regarded for his descriptions of Jesus' narrative pictures. His subjects are all inclined to factual explanations.

Warmth in My Heart (296) 181

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Emerald Bamboo Tears Stain Her Face, Her Heart Breaks; The Fragrance of Red Lotus Fades, A Maiden's Soul Departs

The tigress has always been mindful in her investigation. The master and the coachman are both under her observation. Gengsheng has never revealed any flaws. Today, because of the three words "First Madam," he was caught by her. At that time, it was out of negligence, and there was no room to maneuver. He simply stammered. This madam is like a female judge at home. She could not bear a few words of rebuttal, which made the guilty person's heart tremble with fear. But she knew that if she asked too urgently today, it would be bad and make the other party wary. So, she stopped asking. Two or three days later, the master really went to Hangzhou. The madam called Gengsheng in and said to him in a kind and gentle way, "You called me 'First Madam' the other day. When I asked you, you didn't want to say. But now I already know. I am the First Madam. It turns out that there is another concubine there. That is the master's business. All the criminals who refuse to confess during the interrogation are using some kind of false story or subtle prodding to elicit a natural confession." Gengsheng was flustered by her false report. She said it was a concubine. In Shanghai, the words "concubine" and "second" sound similar. He mistook her for saying "Second Madam." He hurriedly said, "There is no Second Madam." Madam Yin smiled, "Not only a Second Madam, but also a Third Madam." Gengsheng said, "There is indeed no Third Madam." The madam said, "Then there is a Second Madam." Gengsheng said, "This... this..." The madam said, "Don't this that. The master has told me everything. I am not forbidding the master to take a concubine. I just hate him for taking a concubine but hiding it from me. A man with three wives and four concubines, as long as he can afford it, what's the matter? Now he is hiding it from me, which shows that I am not virtuous. So, I have already talked it over with the master. Since he has taken someone, why live outside? It's better to be lively in the mansion. Why borrow a small mansion outside? You don't have to come back in the middle of the night either. You can sleep earlier and save some energy." Gengsheng thought, "Our master repeatedly told me not to tell anyone at home about his taking a concubine and renting a small house, especially not to reveal half a word to the First Madam. How could he tell her first? She is a famous tigress. I think she used some kind of stomach trick or deception to trick the master's words out. Our master is really an honest and upright person. I'm afraid the Second Madam will suffer from now on." Since the master himself has already said it, why should I hide it from her again? He thought like this, which precisely fell into the madam's plan. As the ancients said, "Although I did not kill Bo Ren, Bo Ren died because of me." The life of this Second Madam was lost because of Gengsheng's thinking. It is truly, "Jealousy and madness, night rain destroy flower buds, leaking spring light has willow branches."

If you want to know what happens next, listen to the next chapter.

The Cotton Market Turns Slightly More Stable 189

According to friends in the North and South cotton markets, farmers in the countryside who previously refused to sell are now willing to sell due to the poor situation. However, cotton brokers refuse to buy because factories have no capacity. Cotton brokers have no choice but to stop buying. This situation is rare in recent years. The price of cotton in Shashi, Hubei province, is declining. The previous day, bandits occupied the area, and the tax for one bale of white cotton (approximately 180 catties) was 2 yuan. Now that the military situation is calm, the army has withdrawn, and the bandits have fled, the 2-yuan tax per bale can be canceled, reducing costs for cotton merchants. Goods from the countryside arriving in Hankou are gradually increasing. In another week, arrivals in Shanghai could surge. Yarn Inventory in Shanghai Decreases at the End of September 192

At the end of September, the total yarn inventory in Shanghai factories and yarn warehouses was 113,819 bales, a decrease of 18,305 bales compared to August. The China-British factory had 100,554 bales of yarn, a decrease of 17,425 bales compared to the previous month. Japanese factories had 7,965 bales of yarn, a decrease of 780 bales.

The Downturn in the Grain and Rice Market at Hexia Deepens 193

▲Zhabei: Yesterday, about 50 boats arrived. Sales were even more sluggish. The Changbang new japonica high-grade rice opened at 15.7 yuan in the early morning but dropped to 15.5 yuan by noon, a significant decrease of 0.5 yuan compared to the previous day. Ordinary japonica rice even fell by a staggering 0.7-0.8 yuan. Lower-grade rice opened at just over 13 yuan. The severity of the decline was truly rare. Thin rice was scarce and priced high, but lower-grade rice fell by 0.2 yuan. Sheep glutinous rice and Dushan rice were about to be on par, with prices decreasing by 0.4 yuan each. High-grade sheep glutinous rice opened at just 11.1 yuan. The terminal market was soft by 0.03 yuan, with weak buying interest and an opening price of 11.0 yuan. The source of terminal rice was constant, but sales were slow and transactions were few, with a decline of 0.01-0.02 yuan. Top-grade true glutinous rice was still around 10 yuan. The white yuan market was stable, with no significant changes.

▲South Shanghai: Yesterday, 20-30 boats arrived, and the market on this street was slow. New Changshu and Wuxi japonica rice gradually plummeted by more than 0.5 yuan. Top-grade rice opened at 15.3 yuan, with very few transactions. Suxi groups of white japonica rice faced a severe decline, with high-grade rice falling by 0.3 yuan and mid-grade rice falling by about 0.04 yuan, opening at around 14 yuan. Although the sales of white indica rice and other varieties from the South group were not thriving, due to the arrival of fewer boats, prices only declined by about 0.1 yuan. Sheep glutinous rice remained sluggish. It was difficult to grasp the sales situation. Although there were some sales of Dushan rice, demand was limited. Therefore, street sales were stagnant, and prices fell another 0.3 yuan. High-grade Dushan rice barely opened at 11.5 yuan. Changbang rice remained popular, with high prices still opening at 15.5 yuan. The yin yuan situation was mediocre, with top-grade rice at 14 yuan.

Foreign Rice Still Sells in the North 194

Yesterday, foreign rice was still purchased and loaded by the North China groups, stabilizing the market. 700 bags of No. 1 Saigon rice were sold at 12.5 yuan. Terminal indica rice had sufficient inventory and was affected by the influx of cargo ships. The market continued to decline. Although some Southern groups and merchants from Fujian and Guangdong inquired, prices still fell by more than 0.1 yuan. 1,000 bags of Jiangxi early-season milled rice were sold at prices ranging from 10.025 to 10.9 yuan. 250 bags of milled yuan rice were sold at prices ranging from 14.65 to 14.7 yuan. There were no transactions for other types of rice. Nanjing rice and Anhui brown rice continued to arrive. Although Hunan rice was not scarce, the future situation was still expected to be weak.

Flour and Wheat Market: Near Term Active, Distant Term Flat 195

▲Flour Market: After the opening in the morning, due to slightly better quotations for imported wheat, morale was momentarily boosted, rising by nearly a cent compared to the previous day's closing price. However, in subsequent trading sessions, a pattern of near-term firmness and distant-term weakness emerged. Although the standard for the current month has fallen with the environment, spot goods from various factories still require around 3000 cash, so some manufacturers have been engaging in progressive buying, resulting in a better market atmosphere. Distant months are seeing mainland clients with long positions disregarding market conditions and selling against the trend, so the market remains sluggish. As a result, the current month is up 2.5 li from the previous day, November down 2.5 li, December down 5 li, January down 1 cent, and February/March down 1.25 cents.

▲Wheat Market: After the opening in both the morning and afternoon, the market for each month showed a pattern of near-term firmness and distant-term weakness. The current month is nearing settlement, and bulls, noting that the majority of spot goods on the market are of medium to lower quality, deemed them largely unsuitable for delivery. This has stabilized morale. Although imported wheat prices have improved by 30-40 cents for distant months, most people, feeling unaffected, continue to sell actively. The shorts believe that with imported wheat readily available, local wheat cannot hold its ground, so the market remains slightly down. As a result, the current month is up 2 cents from the previous day, November down 3 cents, December down 4 cents, January/February down 5 cents, and March down 7 cents. Currently, the high-quality wheat market has not opened; only 600 bags of ordinary Zhenjiang wheat have been offered at a price of 3 taels and 900 cash.

Sugar Market: Japanese Sugar Continues to Offer 30,000 Bags

Yesterday's sugar market reports from producing areas indicated that the spot price of Cuban sugar remained at 1.34375, and the price of New York sugar futures for December was 1.34, a decline of 1 cent compared to the previous report. March of the following year was 1.43, down 3 cents; May was 1.49, and September was 1.62, each down 4 cents. The spot price of Java sugar remained at 8.125, and the price of sugar futures for November was 8.00, with no change. The price for December was 8.00, up 0.125 from the previous session. The public market was quiet due to it being Saturday. The transaction price for new cargo of Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse granulated white was 7 taels and 850 cash; new arrivals not yet released were 7 taels and 750 cash, with sparse transactions. Finely ground granulated white was 7 taels and 900 cash, with quiet interest. Dutch No. 8 red sugar was 6 taels and 300 cash, with the market remaining firm. Japanese sugar N mark was offered at 7 taels and 850 cash, and J mark at 8 taels and 100 cash, but there were few inquiries. YT mark was 7 taels and 700 cash, SH mark was 7 taels and 685 cash, and YP mark was 2 taels, with no surprises in the market. Japanese sugar factories continued to offer sugar, with Meiji Sugar offering Japanese gold at 4.55 yuan, for a total of 20,000 bags, and Minghua Sugar at 5.75 yuan, for a total of 10,000 bags, both for December delivery, an increase of 5 cents from the previous offer, with strong demand and a lively market atmosphere. In terms of Dutch sugar disposals, Xiangmao Foreign Firm sold 3,000 bags of No. 24 coarse granulated white for delivery in mid-next month, priced at 5.85 Dutch currency, with the market also quite firm.

North-South Goods: ▲ Dragon Mouth Vermicelli Goods in Short Supply, Preventing Out-of-Stock

▲ Sun-Dried Meat Arrivals Scarce, Expected to Rise

▲ Longkou Vermicelli Noodles: Recently, due to a break in supply, the market has reported out-of-stock conditions, and existing stock is scarce. It will take time for merchants to purchase from the source and ship to Shanghai, so there are concerns of supply disruption. However, due to the small amount of remaining stock, prices have not fluctuated significantly. Yesterday's market price was 20 taels.

▲ Sichuan Pickled Mustard Tuber: Current sales are still good, and the market is stable. Yesterday's market price was 37 yuan for top-quality, around 35 yuan for mid-quality, and 33 yuan for lower-quality.

▲ Xiamen Sun-Dried Longan Meat: Yesterday's investigation revealed that China Merchants Bureau Guangli imported only 11 pieces, making the supply even scarcer than before. Therefore, the market has tightened, with expectations of a rise of approximately 1 to 2 taels.

Seafood: Squid Production Light, Sales Sluggish

A current check of Shanghai's stock of old squid shows only about 300 packages in Tongjie. According to recent reports from producing areas in Japan, the supply of new squid is not as abundant as before, so the source is also becoming scarce. However, sales remain weak, and few goods are being moved. Market quotes from dealers are also unchanged. Currently, whole Qing big-piece box squid is selling for 43 taels, general goods for 41 to 40 taels, and peach squid for 39 taels. Prices for old goods are similar. New No. 2 pair of Zhou squid is 42 to 40 taels and 500 cash, and oil-added slices are 38 to 39 taels. The previous batch of Jinshan squid has already been sold out. Yesterday, a foreign firm sold 50 barrels for delivery in three weeks, priced at 39.5 taels, but dealers showed little interest.

Silk and Tea: European Sales of Chinese Silk Increasingly Lifeless

Yesterday's silk market in Shanghai's foreign firms became increasingly lifeless. Overseas silk sales showed no signs of recovery, and Jiangnan and Zhejiang silk factories were nearly entirely closed. Chinese merchants took a passive stance, and transactions were sparse. Yesterday, only Wei Cheng and others imported 15 packages of Shanghai white factory silk, Jardine Matheson and others imported 20 packages of Sichuan yellow factory silk, and Kechang imported 12 packages of coarse yellow silk, all at flat or weak prices.

New York Japanese Silk Prices Continue to Fall 196

▲ Heavy Stock, Sluggish Sales... Price Falls Another US$0.1-0.2

Since the intrusion of rayon sales and the low-price competition of Japanese silk in the American New York market, silk factory sales have plummeted. Recently, shipments of Japanese silk to the US have continued smoothly, and the stock of silk has increased daily. With autumn sales over, silk factories have sufficient raw materials for winter silk, so silk prices have weakened daily. The price of Japanese silk grade A was only US$2.45 per grade, grade B was US$2, and grade C was US$1.55, each down US$0.1-0.2.

Russian Firms Open for Keemun Black Tea 197

Since Russian firms began purchasing Sui'an Zhenmei tea, British firms have followed suit, and the market has become active. In recent days, both Zhenmei and Gongxi tea have seen brisk transactions. Wuyuan merchants and Jardine Matheson Foreign Firm have also been purchasing in small quantities. The top price offered by Russian firms for Gongxi has already reached 78 taels. Yesterday, Russian firms also earnestly sought to purchase Keemun black tea, and their market offer was significantly more relaxed than before.

Piece Goods: Broadcloth Street Trading is Brisk

Recently, street sales of wool and broadcloth have been extremely brisk. Door-to-door merchants in both the North and South markets have been restocking daily. Goods such as serge, Walter cloth, fancy cloth, and yuan straight cloth are selling well. Clothing merchants, Western tailors, and hat makers are all showing strong interest. Sales of various colors of sea tiger velvet, felt cloth, overcoat cloth, hat cloth, and one-foot-six velvet have continued. The trade association is trending firm, and quoted prices are even more expensive than last week.

Metals: US-Kang Society Iron Sells Well

Recently, new arrivals of US-Kang Society iron from the US-Kang Foreign Firm have been scarce, so the market price has risen by about 2000 cash. It is said that the contents are very large in size and the goods are thin, so all industries and the street are happy to purchase them. As a result, more than 1,000 boxes have been offered in recent days, and various can factories are currently in negotiations for continued purchases.

Black Iron Sheet Reaches Peak 198

Recently, arrivals of black iron sheets have been few, while purchases by various industries have been numerous, and the market supply cannot meet demand, so the market is unusually good. It is currently selling for 11 taels and 250 cash, an increase of 250 cash from before.

Market News 216

▲ Deyu Tongji Flashlight Factory declares that its Ma brand flashlights are novel in style, superior in quality, exquisite in accessories, and extremely low in price. Sales have spread all over the world. Now, for promotion purposes, if electrical material shops and general merchandise stores in various provinces, counties, cities, and towns are willing to distribute these domestic flashlights, the factory will reply to all inquiries. If the distance is remote, the factory has special personnel dedicated to handling shipping procedures.

▲ Huilu Company on Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road announces that its women's clothing department has recently received a large shipment of autumn fabrics, such as printed velvet, which is currently the most popular. There are sixteen different floral patterns, the material is exquisite and very soft. It is 38 inches wide, and about two and a half yards is enough for a fashionable cheongsam. For promotional purposes, the company is selling it for only 11.5 yuan per yard, which is much cheaper than similar products on the market. In addition, there are fine chiffon velvet, with delicate lines and bright colors, in over a hundred varieties, priced from 21.5 yuan to 29.5 yuan. There are also gold and silver satin, with colored flowers on a gold thread base, which are most suitable for making dance costumes and formal dresses, priced from 19.5 yuan to 39.5 yuan. Other items such as fine silk thread and woolen fabrics, colored velvet, etc., are all priced extremely low, making them beautiful and suitable for autumn women's clothing.

▲ Qing Yi Se Restaurant, located at the intersection of Sanma Road and Zhejiang Road, announces that it has recently received the most nourishing big mountain soft-shelled turtles and sea dogfish produced in Guangxi, displayed in the storefront for customers to view. Fresh slaughtering is done every Saturday, paired with local ingredients for stewing, the taste is indeed fresh, sweet, and delicious, with the function of nourishing yin, beautifying the face, and promoting blood circulation. It is a light and nourishing dish that is not greasy, more beneficial than other tonics, and priced extremely low. Furthermore, for promotional purposes, the restaurant has specially improved all kinds of dishes. Whether ordering a full table of dishes or just having a few drinks, all customers will receive special treatment.

▲ Yanhua Restaurant, located opposite Dan Gui Di Yi Tai on Sima Road, announces that its newly added new-style combination dishes, ranging from two yuan to five yuan, all include shark fin, and the dishes are exceptionally rich, with extremely exquisite ingredients. Therefore, it is highly praised by diners. Also, the restaurant's duck liver sausage, rose sausage, osmanthus sausage, gold and silver intestine, duck legs, duck breast, etc., have been very popular since they were launched, and the sales at the storefront have been extremely crowded, especially the duck liver sausage, which has the highest sales volume.

Theater News 217

▲ New Central Theater announces that the film "Tan Deng Yu Yan Ji" (The Story of Tan Deng and the Encounter with Beauty) was shown continuously at the Central Theater for three days and was sold out every day. This film has a unique flavor, and its actions, costumes, and plot are completely non-Chinese. The rugged and desolate river valleys and mountains, the secluded and treacherous treasure caves, as well as the large pythons, crocodiles, monkeys, spiders, and beauties, all make the audience feel a hundred times more interested. Yesterday, the theater opened the film and the audience was even larger. Every show was sold out before it even started, and many of the guests were from the academic community.

▲ Daxin Ticket Office, located at 270 Huile Lane, along Sanma Road, announces that the ticket office was organized by artist Zhang Xinying. Since its establishment, the association has been thriving and nearly sixty members have joined. The hired female role teacher is Fang Yunbiao, the old male role teacher is Shen Shaoting, the zither players are Guo Shucheng and Meng Zhongqing, and the drum player is Xia Yuting. The membership fee is three yuan per month. Requests for membership information will be promptly fulfilled.

▲ Central Grand Theater on Liuma Road announces that it will premiere the latest martial arts romance film, "Dao Ku Qi Yuan" (Strange Fate in the Bandit Cave), directed by Ren Pengnian and starring Wu Lizhu, starting tomorrow (the 8th). Wu Lizhu gives an excellent and brave performance in this film. She has several fierce battles with the gang of thieves, with swords flashing and showing off her skills. Compared to her previous films, the performance has made significant progress.

Youth Forum

Famous Soprano Jovita Fuentes to Perform Tonight 218

Tonight (the 19th) at 9:00 PM, renowned European soprano Jovita Fuentes will hold a concert at the Summer Palace Theatre on Jing'an Temple Road. Ms. Fuentes is an actress from La Scala House in Milan, Italy. She has been welcomed in cities across Europe such as Paris and Berlin. Her name is already on par with the beautiful soprano Galli-Curci. This visit to the Far East for a concert tour was arranged by Mr. A. Strok of this city. She arrived in Shanghai from Manila last week. Tonight's program will include songs from operas such as "Madama Butterfly" and "Iris." It is said that Ms. Fuentes will only perform once in Shanghai tonight. Tickets are priced at five yuan and two and a half yuan. They are sold at the theater. Anyone who studies Western singing should not miss this opportunity.

Music in Universities 219

— Ke Hua

▲ After Listening to the 25th Anniversary Celebration of Fudan University

This time, Fudan University's 25th anniversary celebration actually included a musical performance, which shows that the school does not consider music to be unimportant. In fact, if a university that has been established for 25 years still has no musical organization, I think it would be a shameful thing. Although their performance may not have been perfect, as long as they were able to show their achievements, it showed the spirit of those in charge.

The program included orchestral ensembles, violin solos, ensembles, vocal solos, and choruses. The orchestra performed "Surprise Symphony" (Hey, Gay), "Mignonette", "Caliph of Bagdad", and the Eastern-flavored "Maharajah." Under the baton of the conductor, harmonious melodies flowed out. In particular, the cautious attitude of pianist Ms. Zhou Changming was admirable. According to the instructor, Mr. Lagaspi, "She is indeed a promising talent." In short, all orchestral performances rely on regular practice.

Ye Zantong's violin solo of Chopin's "Serenade" and Wu Shaofu and Peng Qixin's violin ensemble of Elgar's "Salut d'Amour" were both famous violin pieces and were played very movingly. I cannot describe the others in detail. In short, they all had considerable training.

At the same time, I observed the audience and couldn't help but feel doubtful. Westerners place great importance on concerts, dressing in formal attire and never making any noise. However, laughter and chatter filled the theater, and some people even made deliberate booing noises. I cannot help but doubt that the university students in the audience lacked musical cultivation. Therefore, musical education has not yet been fully promoted. Because if one has musical cultivation, they would not have these kinds of habits.

In this way, we must be even more convinced of the importance of music in universities. I believe that in the current universities, in order to promote universal musical education, at least two conditions must be met: First, there must be an orchestra. Second, music courses must be established and given academic credit. Some people may disagree, thinking that there are more important things that have yet to be learned. In fact, there are many scholars in China who regard music as a trivial skill. However, scholars who lead university education, we only see the youth's lives degenerate into indiscipline, transgression, and indulgence in depravity. I hope you can pay attention to it.

Portrait of Ms. Jovita Fuentes 220

About the Fudan University Department of Journalism 221

— Bin

The Purpose Is to Promote Chinese Journalism

Students Are Working Hard on Nationalistic Literature and Art

Among the universities in the country that have established journalism departments, there are only two. The earliest was Yenching University in Beiping. However, their funding relies on the support of American missionaries. Therefore, Chinese students are cultivated into talents for foreign newspapers, instilled with a large amount of religious consciousness, preparing for a kind of anti-propaganda against the Chinese nation in the future. This kind of journalism education with religious aggression, to put it bluntly, is absolutely unnecessary from our nationalistic standpoint. Moreover, no matter how outstanding its achievements may be, it is always considered a great disgrace to our country's educators. Secondly, I want to talk about the Journalism Department of Fudan University.

It is under the jurisdiction of the College of Liberal Arts, so its establishment was after Fudan reformed its university organization in accordance with the Ministry of Education's regulations. Historically, it is naturally very short, only a little over a year. However, the content and organization are very complete, with a great momentum of "surpassing the predecessors." Its purpose is to cultivate specialized talents for the Chinese journalism industry, instill various necessary knowledge, and especially emphasize proficiency in literature and art. The instructors hired are all well-known giants in the domestic journalism field, such as Mr. Ge Gongzhen and Mr. Pan Gongbi. The enthusiasm of Director Xie in handling affairs is also well known to the public. Otherwise, a journalism department that has only been established for a little over a year would never have such achievements.

The department has a total of fifty-four students, most of whom have already achieved considerable honors in society. For example, Deng Youde, a graduate of the last semester, is now a teaching assistant in the College of Liberal Arts of Beiping University and also serves as an editor for the supplements of the Yishi Daily and other newspapers there. Chen Xiliang is responsible for various specialized positions in comparative journalism in this newspaper. Students currently in school, such as Tang Zenghongyang, have already gained considerable honors in the domestic literary and art circles and currently also serve as a professor of Chinese in the preparatory course of the university. Huang Huanruo is a special writer for "Caoye Weekly," the only publication with a nationalistic literary and art center. Wang Deliang is the president of the Fudan News Agency, and Du Bianwen is the editor-in-chief of the Fudan Five-Day Publication. These people are all outstanding talents of the department. Only Zheng Guojing, Wang Rong, Xiong Peifen, Tian Juchang, and Chen Xiangzhong and others were admitted as new students this semester, which shows that the examination of admission results is very strict. According to Mr. Xie Liuyi, the director of the department, the admission of new students this time also paid considerable attention to ideological aspects, so as to avoid the mixing of elements with proletarian consciousness, which would hinder the development of the department. Because the students in the department all admire the nationalistic movement, many have already made considerable achievements in this effort. Recently, the department published a "Fudan University Department of Journalism Commemorative Publication," which is extremely rich in content, with inscriptions from important figures in the party and state and giants in the journalism industry such as Zhu Yingpeng and Zhang Zhuping, and essays by Cheng Tianfang and Qu Wu. From this, one can see the general achievements of the department.

The Shanghai Social Bureau believes that previous national goods movements have not aroused the attention of women, so it initiated the National Goods Fashion Exhibition at the third National Goods Movement this year, which was supported by Shanghai women leaders and the silk industry association, the domestic silk rescue association, and the electrical silk weaving industry association. Pictures of the Chinese Products Pashion Show held under the auspices of the Shanghai District Civic Affairs Bureau in Majestic Hotel on October 9, 193. This was the first show of its kind ever held in China for the purpose encouraging the use of Chinese silk and woollen materials for making ladies dresses and olso introducing new modes in dress-making. Prominent social lender and popular society girls took part or were invited to participate in this unl affair which itself was met with overwhelming success.

(1) Wang Jingqi (X), the Minister to Belgium, and his wife entertained the former Belgian Foreign Minister Fandiwen and his wife and the Belgian Minister Hualuosi and his wife at the Dahua Hotel on October 5.

— (Yang)

(2) The British airship R-101 crashed and exploded on a small mountain in Beauvais, France, on the evening of October 4 while flying to India, killing 46 people. Aviation Minister Thomson was also among them, and only eight people survived. It was the second largest tragedy in aviation history. According to German aviation experts, the British airship was too heavy.

(3) The tide-watching special train on the Hangzhou Road must be transferred to Xiaqiao by small boat to Haining. The sound of oars echoes, and all the noise is gone. The joy of watching the tide is here, not there.

— (M)

(4) The tide-watching venue temporarily built by the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Bureau outside the East Gate of Haining and the tide-watchers.

— (M)

(5) October 8th was the first day of watching the tide in Haining. The tide arrived around 12 noon. The sound of surging waves came from under your feet, and the spray splashed on your clothes. It was a wonderful sight, but the tide head was not very high at first, only about ten feet.

— (M)

(6) The afterwave of the Qiantang tide is silvery and dazzling, with a unique charm.

— (M)
